FROM [AllBeers] AS [a]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[FavoriteBeersId], [b].[FavoriteUsersId], [a0].[Id], [a0].[AccessFailedCount], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[Email], [a0].[EmailConfirmed], [a0].[LockoutEnabled], [a0].[LockoutEnd], [a0].[NormalizedEmail], [a0].[NormalizedUserName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[PhoneNumber], [a0].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a0].[SecurityStamp], [a0].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a0].[UserName]
    FROM [BeerUser] AS [b]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [b].[FavoriteUsersId] = [a0].[Id]
